<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">String Quartet in D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">String Quartet No.34&#160;; "Sun Quartet No.4"
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Haydn,_Joseph" title="Category:Haydn, Joseph">Haydn, Joseph</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/JosephHaydnThematisch-bibliographischesWerkverzeichnis/Hoboken1-3#page/n411/mode/2up">Hob.III:34</a></span>&#160;; Op.20 No.4
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJH 428
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements
<ol><li>Allegro di molto (D major)
</li><li>Un poco adagio affettuoso, with 4 variations (D minor)
</li><li>Minuet. Allegretto alla zingarese - Trio (D major)
</li><li>Presto e scherzando (D major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1772
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1774 in <i><a href="/wiki/String_Quartets,_Op.20_(Haydn,_Joseph)" title="String Quartets, Op.20 (Haydn, Joseph)">String Quartets, Op.20</a></i> (No.4)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Prince Nikolaus Zmeskall von Domanovecz
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical_style" title="Category:Classical style">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>2 violins, viola, cello
</td></tr>
